CANDIDATE 4
generation_source: llm_sql_direct (label: llm_sql_direct)
raw_model_response: SELECT 
    p.patient_id,
    p.first_name,
    p.last_name,
    CAST(SUM(CASE WHEN lt.abnormal_flag = '1' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS REAL) * 100.0 / COUNT(*) AS abnormal_percentage
FROM patients p
JOIN lab_tests lt ON p.patient_id = lt.patient_id
WHERE lt.test_status = 'completed'
GROUP BY p.patient_id, p.first_name, p.last_name
HAVING COUNT(*) > 0;

CANDIDATE 5
generation_source: llm_sql_direct_grain (label: llm_sql_direct_grain)
raw_model_response: SELECT p.patient_id, p.first_name, p.last_name,
       CAST(SUM(CASE WHEN lt.abnormal_flag = '1' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS REAL) * 100.0 /
       NULLIF(SUM(CASE WHEN lt.test_status = 'completed' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END), 0) AS abnormal_percentage
